function set_background_animation
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_bg), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "bg_ani_" & (($idx25 / 32) + 1))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_bg), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ($idx25 mod 32) - ((($idx25 mod 32) - (30 + abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(($idx25 / 32) - 3) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)))) .and. sh_right((30 + abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(($idx25 / 32) - 3) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))) - ($idx25 mod 32), 31)))
end function
function set_key_colors
  $idx25 := 0
  while($idx25 <= 127) 
    set_key_color($idx25, $KEY_COLOR_WHITE)
    if(($idx25 >= 55) and ($idx25 <= 96))
      set_key_color($idx25, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
    end if
    inc($idx25)
  end while
end function
function keyswitches_color_keys
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 7) 
    set_key_color(($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i, $KEY_COLOR_RED)
    if(%_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i] = 1)
      set_key_color(($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i, $KEY_COLOR_ORANGE)
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function update_keyswitch_selection
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 7) 
    set_control_par(%swi_keyswitch[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i])
    set_control_par_str(%lbl_keyswitch[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "          ")
    set_control_par_str(%lbl_keyswitch[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXTLINE, "          ")
    set_control_par_str(%lbl_keyswitch[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXTLINE, !_articulation_names[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i])
    set_control_par(%swi_keyswitch_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_keyswitch_purge_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i])
    set_key_pressed(($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i, %_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i])
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 7) 
    set_key_color(($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i, $KEY_COLOR_RED)
    if(%_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i] = 1)
      set_key_color(($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i, $KEY_COLOR_ORANGE)
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $selected_subarticulation := 0
  if(get_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_editor_page), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE) = $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    $idx25 := $idx25
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_editor_page), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_articulation_humanize), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_humanization[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_articulation_humanize), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_articulation_humanize & " ms")
    if(%_articulation_release[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch] >= 0)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_articulation_release), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_release[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_articulation_release), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_articulation_release & " ms")
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_articulation_release_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      $btn_articulation_release := 0
    else
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_articulation_release), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "")
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_articulation_release_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      $btn_articulation_release := 1
    end if
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_min), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_max), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch] * -1)
    $i := 0
    while($i <= (num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope) - 1)) 
      set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, int(round(real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) + (real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.) - int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) * pow(real($i) / real(num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope)), (real(%_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 100.) + 1.)))))
      set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) - get_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
      inc($i)
    end while
    $subarticulation_event1 := $idx25
    $group_count001 := $selected_subarticulation
    $group_count000 := $idx25
    $idx25 := 0
    while($idx25 <= (num_elements(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection) - 1)) 
      if($idx25 # $group_count001)
        set_control_par(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[$idx25], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
      else
        set_control_par(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[$idx25], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
      end if
      inc($idx25)
    end while
    if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] # -1)
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_title), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "    " & !subarticulations_full_name[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]])
    else
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_title), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "    Empty")
    end if
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_solo_subarticulation), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_subarticulations_solo_states[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulations_volume[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_volume & " dB")
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_subarticulation_repetition_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_repetition_speed_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_subarticulation_rr_mode), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_rr_mode_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    if(((%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 0) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 5)) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 6))
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulations_tightness[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_tightness & " %")
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      $mnu_subarticulation_rr_mode := %_loaded_subarticulations_rr_mode[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_subarticulation_rr_mode), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_rr_mode_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    end if
    if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 6)
      $mnu_subarticulation_repetition_speed := %_loaded_subarticulations_repetition_speed[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_subarticulation_repetition_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_repetition_speed_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    end if
    if(((%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 1) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 2)) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 4))
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulations_vibrato[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_vibrato & " %")
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    end if
    if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 2)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulations_trans_volume[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_trans_volume & " dB")
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulation_trans_speed[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_trans_speed & " %")
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      $btn_subarticulation_trans_speed := %_loaded_subarticulation_trans_speed_auto[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      if($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed = 1)
        set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      end if
    end if
    $i := 0
    while($i <= 3) 
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)] # -1)
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        if($i = $selected_subarticulation)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-selected-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-left-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-right-" & $i)
        else
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-unselected-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-left-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-right-" & $i)
        end if
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, 127 - %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
      end if
      inc($i)
    end while
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] + %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] - %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(-200. + ((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * 200.))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(round((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0]) * 200.))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]) * 200.))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    ?xy_dynamic_range[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_dynamic_range[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[0] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
    $group_count001 := %modulation_positions[0]
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_cursor), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 5) + int((real((($group_count001 * (1 + (sh_right(127 - $group_count001, 31) .or. sh_right($group_count001 - 1, 31)))) - sh_right($group_count001 - 1, 31)) - (127 * sh_right(127 - $group_count001, 31))) / 127.) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))))
    @txt_keyswitch_name := !_articulation_names[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_min), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_max), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch] * -1)
    $i := 0
    while($i <= (num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope) - 1)) 
      set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, int(round(real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) + (real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.) - int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) * pow(real($i) / real(num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope)), (real(%_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 100.) + 1.)))))
      set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) - get_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
      inc($i)
    end while
    $i := 0
    while($i <= 3) 
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)] # -1)
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        if($i = $selected_subarticulation)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-selected-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-left-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-right-" & $i)
        else
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-unselected-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-left-" & $i)
          set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-right-" & $i)
        end if
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
        set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, 127 - %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
      end if
      inc($i)
    end while
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] + %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] - %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(-200. + ((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * 200.))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(round((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0]) * 200.))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]) * 200.))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    ?xy_dynamic_range[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    ?xy_dynamic_range[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[0] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
    $group_count001 := %modulation_positions[0]
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_cursor), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 5) + int((real((($group_count001 * (1 + (sh_right(127 - $group_count001, 31) .or. sh_right($group_count001 - 1, 31)))) - sh_right($group_count001 - 1, 31)) - (127 * sh_right(127 - $group_count001, 31))) / 127.) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))))
    if(get_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_subarticulation_browser), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE) = $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      $idx25 := $idx25
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_subarticulation_browser), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] # -1)
        $idx25 := %type_to_category[%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]]]
        $subarticulation_event1 := 0
        while($subarticulation_event1 <= (num_elements(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection) - 1)) 
          set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
          if(%_subarticulation_browser_entries[($idx25 * 14) + $subarticulation_event1] # -1)
            set_control_par_str(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !subarticulations_full_name[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_subarticulation_browser_entries[($idx25 * 14) + $subarticulation_event1]]])
            if(%_subarticulation_browser_entries[($idx25 * 14) + $subarticulation_event1] = %_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
              set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
            else
              set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
            end if
            set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
          end if
          inc($subarticulation_event1)
        end while
        $subarticulation_event1 := 0
        while($subarticulation_event1 <= (num_elements(%btn_subarticulation_browser_category) - 1)) 
          if($subarticulation_event1 = $idx25)
            set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_category[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
          else
            set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_category[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
          end if
          inc($subarticulation_event1)
        end while
        $subarticulation_browser_active_category := $idx25
      end if
    end if
  end if
end function
function keyswitches_on_note
  $fade_out_range01 := 0
  $subarticulation_event1 := 0
  if(in_range($transition_note_event00, $keyswitch_octave * 12, (($keyswitch_octave * 12) + 8) - 1))
    $i := 0
    while($i <= 7) 
      $fade_out_range01 := %_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i]
      %_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i] := %KEY_DOWN[($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i]
      if($fade_out_range01 # %_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i])
        $subarticulation_event1 := 1
      end if
      $selected_keyswitch := $transition_note_event00 - ($keyswitch_octave * 12)
      inc($i)
    end while
    if($subarticulation_event1 = 1)
      $transition_note_event00 := $idx25
      call update_keyswitch_selection
    end if
  end if
end function
function wait_or_zero
  if(%wait_time0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] > 0)
    wait(%wait_time0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100])
  end if
end function
function is_in_note_selection
  $i1300 := 0
  select($result1500)
    case 0
      $i1300 := 1
    case 1
      $i1300 := - sh_right(abs($offset10) - 1, 31)
    case 2
      $i1300 := - sh_right(abs($offset10) - 1, 31) + - sh_right(abs($offset10 - 1) - 1, 31)
    case 3
      $i1300 := (- sh_right(abs($offset10) - 1, 31) + (- sh_right(abs($offset10 - ($_ret4000 / 2)) - 1, 31) * (1 + sh_right(3 - $_ret4000, 31)))) + (- sh_right(abs($offset10 - (($_ret4000 / 2) - 1)) - 1, 31) * - sh_right(3 - $_ret4000, 31))
    case 4
      $i1300 := (- sh_right(abs($offset10) - 1, 31) + (- sh_right(abs($offset10 - ($_ret4000 / 2)) - 1, 31) * (1 + sh_right(3 - $_ret4000, 31)))) + (- sh_right(abs($offset10 - ((($_ret4000 - 1) / 2) + 1)) - 1, 31) * - sh_right(3 - $_ret4000, 31))
    case 5
      $i1300 := - sh_right(abs($offset10 - ($_ret4000 / 2)) - 1, 31)
    case 6
      $i1300 := (((- sh_right(abs($offset10 - ($_ret4000 / 2)) - 1, 31) * (1 + sh_right(3 - $_ret4000, 31))) + (- sh_right(abs($offset10 - (($_ret4000 / 2) - 1)) - 1, 31) * - sh_right(3 - $_ret4000, 31))) + (- sh_right(abs($offset10 - $_ret4000) - 1, 31) * (1 + sh_right(3 - ($_ret4000 + 1), 31)))) + (- sh_right(abs($offset10 - (((($_ret4000 + 1) - 1) / 2) + 1)) - 1, 31) * - sh_right(3 - ($_ret4000 + 1), 31))
    case 7
      $i1300 := (- sh_right(abs($offset10 - ($_ret4000 / 2)) - 1, 31) * (1 + sh_right(3 - $_ret4000, 31))) + (- sh_right(abs($offset10 - (($_ret4000 / 2) - 1)) - 1, 31) * - sh_right(3 - $_ret4000, 31))
    case 8
      $i1300 := (- sh_right(abs($offset10 - ($_ret4000 / 2)) - 1, 31) * (1 + sh_right(3 - $_ret4000, 31))) + (- sh_right(abs($offset10 - ((($_ret4000 - 1) / 2) + 1)) - 1, 31) * - sh_right(3 - $_ret4000, 31))
    case 9
      $i1300 := - sh_right(abs($offset10 - ($_ret4000 - 1)) - 1, 31)
    case 10
      $i1300 := - sh_right(abs($offset10 - ($_ret4000 - 1)) - 1, 31) + - sh_right(abs($offset10 - ($_ret4000 - 2)) - 1, 31)
    case 11

                                end if
                              end if
                            end if
                          end if
                          inc($string0200)
                        end while
                      end if
                    end if
                    inc($ii100)
                  end while
                end if
              end if
            end if
          end if
        end if
        inc($event100)
      end while
      if($i1400 = 1)
        $group_count001 := $reduced_note01
        $iii1 := $ret14

        $_ret6600 := $octave_event000
        call event_list_add_articulation_event
        $group_count001 := 0
        $_ret6600 := $_ret570
        $iii1 := $ii100
        $ii4 := $string0200
        call note_to_string
        $transition_dyn_layer00 := $group_count000
        %_last_articulation_event[($reduced_note01 * 1024) + (($ret14 * 128) + ($transition_dyn_layer00 * $allow_double_stops))] := $octave_event000
        %_last_articulation_event[($reduced_note01 * 1024) + (($ret14 * 128) + $_ret570)] := $octave_event000
      end if
    end if

  end while
end function

function update_selected_notes
  $i11000 := 0
  $pressed_key_idx := 0
  $i := 127
  while($i >= 0) 
    if(%pressed_keys[$i] > ($ENGINE_UPTIME - $input_acceptance_time))
      $inst := 0
      while($inst <= 0) 
        $offset10 := ($num_pressed_keys - 1) - $pressed_key_idx
        $_ret4000 := $num_pressed_keys
        $result1500 := %note_selections[$inst]
        $i1200 := $i1300
        call is_in_note_selection
        if($is_in_note_selection_boolean = 1)
          %_pressed_notes_per_instrument[($inst * 128) + $i] := 1
          $reduced_note01 := $inst
          $_ret570 := $i
          $i14 := %key_velocity[$i]
          $i17 := %pressed_keys[$i] - $ENGINE_UPTIME
          $ret14 := $i1300
          $subarticulation_id0 := $event100
          $group_count0 := $octave_event000
          $subarticulation_id1 := $i1400
          $purge_state0 := $ii100
          $_ret660 := $_ret57000
          $group_count00 := $reduced_note0100
          $string020 := $string0200
          $reduced_note010 := $transition_dyn_layer00
          $_ret5700 := $transition_type20
          $ii10 := $transition_note00
          $i140 := $end_note20
          $octave_event00 := $idx2300
          $i130 := $i150
          call articulations_on_note
          $string0100 := $string010
          $ii20 := $event10
        else
          %_pressed_notes_per_instrument[($inst * 128) + $i] := 0
          $i130 := $inst
          $event10 := $i
          $octave_event00 := $i1300
          $i140 := $octave_event000
          $ii10 := $i1400
          $reduced_note010 := $ii100
          $string010 := $_ret57000
          $string020 := $idx2300
          $group_count00 := $transition_dyn_layer00
          $_ret660 := $string0200
          $purge_state0 := $event100
          $subarticulation_id1 := $transition_type20
          $group_count0 := $transition_note00
          $subarticulation_id0 := $end_note20
          call articulations_note_off
          $reduced_note0100 := $_ret5700
        end if
        inc($inst)
      end while
    else
      if(%pressed_keys[$i] > 0)
        $inst := 0
        while($inst <= 0) 
          $offset10 := ($num_pressed_keys - 1) - $pressed_key_idx
          $_ret4000 := $num_pressed_keys
          $result1500 := %note_selections[$inst]
          $i1200 := $end_note20
          call is_in_note_selection
          if($is_in_note_selection_boolean = 0)
            $i130 := $inst
            $event10 := $i
            $octave_event00 := $end_note20
            $i140 := $transition_note00
            $ii10 := $transition_type20
            $reduced_note010 := $string0200
            $string010 := $transition_dyn_layer00
            $string020 := $idx2300
            $group_count00 := $_ret57000
            $_ret660 := $ii100
            $purge_state0 := $reduced_note0100
            $subarticulation_id1 := $i1400
            $group_count0 := $octave_event000
            $subarticulation_id0 := $i1300
            call articulations_note_off
            $event100 := $_ret5700
            %_pressed_notes_per_instrument[($inst * 128) + $i] := 0
          end if
          inc($inst)
        end while
      end if
    end if
    if(%pressed_keys[$i] > 0)
      inc($pressed_key_idx)
    end if
    dec($i)
  end while
  $inst := 0
  while($inst <= 0) 
    %active_notes[$inst] := 0
    $i := 0
    while($i <= 127) 
      if(%_pressed_notes_per_instrument[($inst * 128) + $i] = 1)
        inc(%active_notes[$inst])
      end if
      inc($i)
    end while
    inc($inst)
  end while
end function

function articulations_compute_level
  ~subarticulation_modulation_strength01 := 0.
  $i1200 := %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($group_count0 * 32) + (($subarticulation_id1 * 4) + $_ret660)]
  $result1500 := %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($group_count0 * 32) + (($subarticulation_id1 * 4) + $_ret660)]
  $_ret4000 := %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($group_count0 * 32) + (($subarticulation_id1 * 4) + $_ret660)]
  $offset10 := %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($group_count0 * 32) + (($subarticulation_id1 * 4) + $_ret660)]
  if(in_range(%modulation_positions[$purge_state0 * $use_polyphonic_modulation], $i1200, $_ret4000))
    ~subarticulation_modulation_strength01 := 1.
    if(in_range(%modulation_positions[$purge_state0 * $use_polyphonic_modulation], $i1200, $i1200 + $result1500) and ($result1500 > 0))
      ~subarticulation_modulation_strength01 := real(%modulation_positions[$purge_state0 * $use_polyphonic_modulation] - $i1200) / real($result1500)
    else
      if(in_range(%modulation_positions[$purge_state0 * $use_polyphonic_modulation], $_ret4000 - $offset10, $_ret4000) and ($offset10 > 0))
        ~subarticulation_modulation_strength01 := real($_ret4000 - %modulation_positions[$purge_state0 * $use_polyphonic_modulation]) / real($offset10)
      end if
    end if
  end if
  $subarticulation_id0 := int(1000000. * ((real(int(round(real(%_articulation_volume_min[($group_count0 * 8) + $subarticulation_id1]) + (real(%_articulation_volume_max[($group_count0 * 8) + $subarticulation_id1] - %_articulation_volume_min[($group_count0 * 8) + $subarticulation_id1]) * pow(real(%modulation_positions[$purge_state0 * $use_polyphonic_modulation]) / 127., (real(%_articulation_volume_curve[($group_count0 * 8) + $subarticulation_id1]) / 100.) + 1.))))) / 127.) * ~subarticulation_modulation_strength01))
end function
function subarticulation_set_level
  $_ret6600 := $string02

  $ii4 := $group_count000

  if(%subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[$string02] # -1)
    set_event_par_arr(%subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[$string02], $EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, $group_count000, 2)
    if(%subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[$string02] # -1)
      set_event_par_arr(%subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[$string02], $EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, $group_count000, 2)
    end if
  end if
  %subarticulation_event_level[$string02] := $group_count000
end function

function get_next_rr
  $i150 := 0
  if(%subarticulations_rrr[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($ii4 * 32) + (($string02 * 4) + $group_count000)]]] = 0)
    if(%_loaded_subarticulations_rr_mode[($ii4 * 32) + (($string02 * 4) + $group_count000)] = 0)
      $i150 := (%_rr_data_idx[($ii4 * 4096) + (($string02 * 512) + (($group_count000 * 128) + $group_count001))] + 1) mod %subarticulations_rr_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($ii4 * 32) + (($string02 * 4) + $group_count000)]]]
    else
      $i150 := random(0, %subarticulations_rr_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($ii4 * 32) + (($string02 * 4) + $group_count000)]]] - 1)
    end if
  else
    if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - %_rr_data_time[($ii4 * 4096) + (($string02 * 512) + (($group_count000 * 128) + $group_count001))]) > %subarticulations_rrr_reset_time[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($ii4 * 32) + (($string02 * 4) + $group_count000)]]])
      if(%_loaded_subarticulations_rr_mode[($ii4 * 32) + (($string02 * 4) + $group_count000)] = 0)
        $i150 := (%_rr_data_idx[($ii4 * 4096) + (($string02 * 512) + (($group_count000 * 128) + $group_count001))] + 1) mod %subarticulations_rrr[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($ii4 * 32) + (($string02 * 4) + $group_count000)]]]
      else
        $i150 := random(0, %subarticulations_rrr[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($ii4 * 32) + (($string02 * 4) + $group_count000)]]] - 1)
      end if
    else
      if(%_loaded_subarticulations_rr_mode[($ii4 * 32) + (($string02 * 4) + $group_count000)] = 0)
        $i150 := %subarticulations_rrr[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($ii4 * 32) + (($string02 * 4) + $group_count000)]]] - ((%subarticulations_rrr[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($ii4 * 32) + (($string02 * 4) + $group_count000)]]] - ((%_rr_data_idx[($ii4 * 4096) + (($string02 * 512) + (($group_count000 * 128) + $group_count001))] + 1) mod %subarticulations_rr_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($ii4 * 32) + (($string02 * 4) + $group_count000)]]])) .and. sh_right(%subarticulations_rrr[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($ii4 * 32) + (($string02 * 4) + $group_count000)]]] - ((%_rr_data_idx[($ii4 * 4096) + (($string02 * 512) + (($group_count000 * 128) + $group_count001))] + 1) mod %subarticulations_rr_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($ii4 * 32) + (($string02 * 4) + $group_count000)]]]), 31))
      else
        $i150 := random(%subarticulations_rrr[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($ii4 * 32) + (($string02 * 4) + $group_count000)]]], %subarticulations_rr_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($ii4 * 32) + (($string02 * 4) + $group_count000)]]] - 1)
      end if
    end if
    %_rr_data_time[($ii4 * 4096) + (($string02 * 512) + (($group_count000 * 128) + $group_count001))] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  end if
  %_rr_data_idx[($ii4 * 4096) + (($string02 * 512) + (($group_count000 * 128) + $group_count001))] := $i150
  $result150 := $i150
end function
function subarticulation_event_get_free_index
  $idx2300 := -1
  $ii20 := 0
  while($ii20 < 128) 
    if((%subarticulation_event_list[$ii20] = -1) and (%subarticulation_event_last_used[$ii20] < ($ENGINE_UPTIME - $lookahead)))
      $idx2300 := $ii20
      $ii20 := 128
    end if
    $ii20 := $ii20 + 1
  end while
  $ii4 := $idx2300
end function

function subarticulation_event_fade_out
  if(abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%subarticulation_event_list[$group_count001] - -1) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)) = 1)
    fade_out(%subarticulation_event_list[$group_count001], $_ret6600 * 1000, $group_count000)
    if(abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%subarticulation_event_octave_layer_id[$group_count001] - -1) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)) = 1)
      fade_out(%subarticulation_event_octave_layer_id[$group_count001], $_ret6600 * 1000, $group_count000)
    end if
    if(%subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[$group_count001] # -1)
      fade_out(%subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[$group_count001], $_ret6600 * 1000, $group_count000)
    end if
    if(%subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[$group_count001] # -1)
      fade_out(%subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[$group_count001], $_ret6600 * 1000, $group_count000)
    end if
    if($group_count000 = 1)
      $ii4 := $group_count001
      $iii1 := -1
      call subarticulation_event_set_event_id
    end if
  end if
end function
function subarticulation_octave_layer_set_event_id
  %subarticulation_event_octave_layer_id[$iii1] := $ii4
end function
function subarticulation_event_set_event_mark
  if(abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%subarticulation_event_list[$ii4] - -1) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)) = 1)
    set_event_mark(%subarticulation_event_list[$ii4], $group_count001)
    if(abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%subarticulation_event_octave_layer_id[$ii4] - -1) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)) = 1)
      set_event_mark(%subarticulation_event_octave_layer_id[$ii4], $group_count001)
    end if
  end if
end function
function subarticulation_event_disallow_groups
  $_ret6600 := $group_count001
  $iii1 := $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP
  $ii4 := 0
  $group_count001 := $ALL_GROUPS
  call subarticulation_event_set_event_par_arr
end function
function subarticulation_event_allow_groups
  $_ret6600 := $group_count001
  $iii1 := $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP
  $ii4 := 1
  $group_count001 := 1
  call subarticulation_event_set_event_par_arr
end function
function subarticulation_event_change_vol
  if(abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%subarticulation_event_list[$group_count001] - -1) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)) = 1)
    change_vol(%subarticulation_event_list[$group_count001], $ii4, $iii1)
    if(abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%subarticulation_event_octave_layer_id[$group_count001] - -1) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)) = 1)
      change_vol(%subarticulation_event_octave_layer_id[$group_count001], $ii4, $iii1)
    end if
  end if
end function
function subarticulation_event_fade_in
  if(abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%subarticulation_event_list[$group_count000] - -1) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)) = 1)
    fade_in(%subarticulation_event_list[$group_count000], $_ret6600 * 1000)
    if(abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%subarticulation_event_octave_layer_id[$group_count000] - -1) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)) = 1)
      fade_in(%subarticulation_event_octave_layer_id[$group_count000], $_ret6600 * 1000)
    end if
    if(%subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[$group_count000] # -1)
      fade_in(%subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[$group_count000], $_ret6600 * 1000)
    end if
    if(%subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[$group_count000] # -1)
      fade_in(%subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[$group_count000], $_ret6600 * 1000)
    end if
  end if
end function
function repetition_engine_add
  $group_count001 := search(%repetition_engine_subarticulation_events, -1)
  if($group_count001 # -1)
    %repetition_engine_subarticulation_events[$group_count001] := $iii1
    $repetition_engine_active := 1
    if($repetition_engine_start_time = -1)
      $repetition_engine_start_time := $ENGINE_UPTIME
    end if
  else
    message("REACHED MAX_SUBARTICULATIONS_IN_REPETITION_ENGINE")
  end if
end function
function update_authoring_labels
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_sustain_release), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_sustain_release & " + " & $sli_sustain_release_offset & " ms")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_trans_start), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_trans_start & " + " & $sli_trans_start_offset & " ms")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_trans_fadeIn), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, int((real($sli_trans_fadeIn) / 1000000.) * 750.) & " + " & int((real($sli_trans_fadeIn_offset) / 1000000.) * 750.) & " ms")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, (round((real($sli_trans_volume) / 1000.) * pow(10., 2.)) / pow(10., 2.)) & " + " & (round((real($sli_trans_volume_offset) / 1000.) * pow(10., 2.)) / pow(10., 2.)) & " dB")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_trans_fadeOut), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, int((real($sli_trans_fadeOut) / 1000000.) * 1000.) & " + " & int((real($sli_trans_fadeOut_offset) / 1000000.) * 1000.) & " ms")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_sustain_wait), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, int((real($sli_sustain_wait) / 1000000.) * 500.) & " + " & int((real($sli_sustain_wait_offset) / 1000000.) * 500.) & " ms")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_sustain_fadeIn), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, int((real($sli_sustain_fadeIn) / 1000000.) * 500.) & " + " & int((real($sli_sustain_fadeIn_offset) / 1000000.) * 500.) & " ms")
end function

      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_sustain_wait), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_legato_data_sus_wait_time[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + (abs($subarticulation_event1 - $idx25) + (- sh_right(- ($subarticulation_event1 - $idx25), 31) * 12)))])
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_sustain_fadeIn), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_legato_data_sus_fade_in_time[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + (abs($subarticulation_event1 - $idx25) + (- sh_right(- ($subarticulation_event1 - $idx25), 31) * 12)))])

      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_trans_start_offset), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_legato_data_trans_zone_start_offset[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + (abs($subarticulation_event1 - $idx25) + (- sh_right(- ($subarticulation_event1 - $idx25), 31) * 12)))])

      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_trans_fadeOut_offset), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_legato_data_trans_fade_out_time_offset[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + (abs($subarticulation_event1 - $idx25) + (- sh_right(- ($subarticulation_event1 - $idx25), 31) * 12)))])

function last_transitions_update
  $i11000 := 0
  while($i11000 <= (num_elements(%_last_transitions) - 1)) 
    if(%_last_transitions[$i11000] # -1)
      if(%_last_transitions_timecode[$i11000] < ($ENGINE_UPTIME - 2000))
        %_last_transitions[$i11000] := -1
      end if
    end if
    inc($i11000)
  end while
end function
function last_transitions_contains
  $event100 := 0
  $ii1 := $i11000
  call last_transitions_update
  $i1300 := 0
  while($i1300 <= 7) 
    if(%_last_transitions[($reduced_note01 * 256) + (($string01 * 32) + (($_ret6600 * 8) + $i1300))] = ((128 * $iii1) + $group_count001))
      $event100 := 1
      %_last_transitions[($reduced_note01 * 256) + (($string01 * 32) + (($_ret6600 * 8) + $i1300))] := -1
    end if
    inc($i1300)
  end while
  $_ret570 := $event100
end function
function last_transitions_add_event
  $_ret6600 := -1
  $string01 := %_last_transitions_timecode[($ii4 * 256) + (($string02 * 32) + ($group_count000 * 8))]
  $reduced_note01 := 0
  $_ret4000 := 0
  if($group_count001 >= 0)
    $_ret4000 := 0
    while($_ret4000 <= 7) 
      if(%_last_transitions[($ii4 * 256) + (($string02 * 32) + (($group_count000 * 8) + $_ret4000))] = -1)
        $_ret6600 := $_ret4000
        if($string01 > %_last_transitions_timecode[($ii4 * 256) + (($string02 * 32) + (($group_count000 * 8) + $_ret4000))])
          $string01 := %_last_transitions_timecode[($ii4 * 256) + (($string02 * 32) + (($group_count000 * 8) + $_ret4000))]
          $reduced_note01 := $_ret4000
        end if
      end if
      inc($_ret4000)
    end while
    if($_ret6600 # -1)
      %_last_transitions[($ii4 * 256) + (($string02 * 32) + (($group_count000 * 8) + $_ret6600))] := (128 * $group_count001) + $iii1
      %_last_transitions_timecode[($ii4 * 256) + (($string02 * 32) + (($group_count000 * 8) + $_ret6600))] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
    else
      %_last_transitions[($ii4 * 256) + (($string02 * 32) + (($group_count000 * 8) + $reduced_note01))] := (128 * $group_count001) + $iii1
      %_last_transitions_timecode[($ii4 * 256) + (($string02 * 32) + (($group_count000 * 8) + $reduced_note01))] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
    end if
  end if
end function
function repetition_engine_remove
  $group_count001 := search(%repetition_engine_subarticulation_events, $subarticulation_event1)
  if($group_count001 # -1)
    %repetition_engine_subarticulation_events[$group_count001] := -1
  end if
end function
function subarticulation_note_off
  if(abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%subarticulation_event_list[$_ret6600] - -1) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)) = 1)
    $group_count000 := %subarticulation_event_subarticulation[$_ret6600]
    $subarticulation_event1 := $_ret6600
    $idx25 := $group_count001
    call repetition_engine_remove
    if((%subarticulations_release_time[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count000]] = 0) or (($ENGINE_UPTIME - %last_pressed[%subarticulation_event_note[$_ret6600]]) < %subarticulations_release_time[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count000]]))
      $group_count001 := %_articulation_release[(%articulation_event_instrument[%subarticulation_event_articulation_event[$_ret6600]] * 8) + %articulation_event_keyswitch[%subarticulation_event_articulation_event[$_ret6600]]]
      if($group_count001 >= 0)
        $group_count001 := $_ret6600
        $_ret6600 := $group_count001
        $group_count000 := 1
        call subarticulation_event_fade_out
      else
        if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count000]] = 2)
          $group_count001 := 300
          $group_count001 := $_ret6600
          $_ret6600 := $group_count001
          $group_count000 := 1
          call subarticulation_event_fade_out
        else
          note_off(%subarticulation_event_list[$_ret6600])
          if(%subarticulation_event_octave_layer_id[$_ret6600] # -1)
            note_off(%subarticulation_event_octave_layer_id[$_ret6600])
          end if
        end if
      end if
      if((%subarticulations_release_group[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count000]] = 1) and (($authoring_page_active = 0) or ($btn_play_sustain = 1)))
        $offset10 := play_note(%subarticulation_event_note[$_ret6600], %key_velocity[%subarticulation_event_note[$_ret6600]], 0, 0)
        $transition_octave_event00 := -1
        if(%subarticulation_event_octave_layer[$_ret6600] # 0)
          $transition_octave_event00 := play_note(%subarticulation_event_note[$_ret6600] + 12, %key_velocity[%subarticulation_event_note[$_ret6600]], 0, 0)
        end if
        $ii4 := $_ret6600
        $iii1 := $offset10
        call subarticulation_event_set_event_id
        $iii1 := $_ret6600
        $ii4 := $transition_octave_event00
        call subarticulation_octave_layer_set_event_id
        $group_count001 := $_ret6600
        call subarticulation_event_disallow_groups
        $fade_out_range01 := 0
        $transition_note_event00 := 0
        while($transition_note_event00 <= (%subarticulations_dynamic_layers[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count000]] - 1)) 
          $fade_out_range01 := 0
          while($fade_out_range01 <= 5) 
            if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count000]] # 2)
              $group_count001 := $_ret6600
              $ii4 := (((%subarticulations_group_idx[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count000]] + 1) + (((6 * %subarticulations_rr_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count000]]) * %subarticulations_dynamic_layers[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count000]]) * (%subarticulation_event_interval[$_ret6600] * 2))) + ((($transition_note_event00 * (%subarticulations_release_group[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count000]] + 1)) + 1) * 6)) + $fade_out_range01
              call subarticulation_event_allow_groups
            else
              $group_count001 := $_ret6600
              $ii4 := (((%subarticulations_group_idx[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count000]] + 1) + (6 * ((%subarticulations_dynamic_layers[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count000]] * 2) + %subarticulations_trans_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count000]]))) + ($transition_note_event00 * 6)) + $fade_out_range01
              call subarticulation_event_allow_groups
            end if
            inc($fade_out_range01)
          end while
          inc($transition_note_event00)
        end while
        $group_count000 := $_ret6600
        $string02 := %subarticulation_event_modulation[$_ret6600]
        call subarticulation_set_modulation
        $string02 := $_ret6600
        $group_count000 := %subarticulation_event_level[$_ret6600]
        call subarticulation_set_level
        if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count000]] = 2)
          $group_count001 := 0
          $_ret6600 := %subarticulation_event_note[$_ret6600]
          $iii1 := $fade_in_range01
          $ii4 := $fade_in_start01
          call note_to_string
          $fade_out_end01 := $group_count000
          %_release_per_string[(%articulation_event_instrument[%subarticulation_event_articulation_event[$_ret6600]] * 8) + ($fade_out_end01 * 2)] := $offset10
          $group_count001 := 0
          $_ret6600 := %subarticulation_event_note[$_ret6600]
          $iii1 := $fade_in_start01
          $ii4 := $rr10
          call note_to_string
          $fade_in_range01 := $group_count000
          %_release_per_string[(%articulation_event_instrument[%subarticulation_event_articulation_event[$_ret6600]] * 8) + (($fade_in_range01 * 2) + 1)] := $transition_octave_event00
        end if
      end if
    end if
    $ii4 := $_ret6600
    $iii1 := -1
    call subarticulation_event_set_event_id
    $iii1 := $_ret6600
    $ii4 := -1
    call subarticulation_octave_layer_set_event_id
  end if
  %subarticulation_event_note[$_ret6600] := -1
  %subarticulation_event_actual_note[$_ret6600] := -1
  %subarticulation_event_subarticulation[$_ret6600] := -1
  %subarticulation_event_modulation[$_ret6600] := -1
  %subarticulation_event_level[$_ret6600] := -1
  %subarticulation_event_interval[$_ret6600] := 0
  %subarticulation_event_last_used[$_ret6600] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  %subarticulation_event_articulation_event[$_ret6600] := -1
  %subarticulation_event_subarticulation_idx[$_ret6600] := -1
end function
function subarticulation_play_note
  $iii1 := $ii20
  $_ret6600 := $idx2300
  call subarticulation_event_get_free_index
  $subarticulation_event_id18 := $ii4
  $ii20 := 0
  $idx2300 := -1
  $end_note20 := -1
  $transition_note00 := -1
  $transition_type20 := 0
  $transition_dyn_layer00 := 0
  if(($subarticulation_event_id18 # -1) and ($subarticulation_id1 # -1))
    if(($subarticulations_solo_states_any_active = 0) or (%_subarticulations_solo_states[($_ret660 * 32) + (($purge_state0 * 4) + $subarticulation_id1)] = 1))
      if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count0]] # 2)
        $ii20 := play_note($subarticulation_id0 + $transpose0, $ret14, ((%subarticulations_start_offset[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count0]] - 10) * 1000) * abs(sh_right(abs($use_constant_delay) - 1, 31)), 0)
        if($octave_layer0 # 0)
          $idx2300 := play_note(($subarticulation_id0 + $transpose0) + (12 * $octave_layer0), $ret14, ((%subarticulations_start_offset[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count0]] - 10) * 1000) * abs(sh_right(abs($use_constant_delay) - 1, 31)), 0)
        end if
        if((((%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count0]] = 0) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count0]] = 3)) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count0]] = 5)) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count0]] = 6))
          if($previous_note0 >= 0)
            if((%articulation_event_instrument[%subarticulation_event_articulation_event[$previous_note0]] = $_ret660) and (%articulation_event_keyswitch[%subarticulation_event_articulation_event[$previous_note0]] = $purge_state0))
              $group_count001 := $previous_note0
              $_ret6600 := 1000 - int((700. * real(%_loaded_subarticulations_tightness[($_ret660 * 32) + (($purge_state0 * 4) + $subarticulation_id1)])) / 100.)
              $group_count000 := 1
              call subarticulation_event_fade_out
            end if
          end if
        end if
        $ii4 := $subarticulation_event_id18
        $iii1 := $ii20
        call subarticulation_event_set_event_id
        $iii1 := $subarticulation_event_id18
        $ii4 := $idx2300
        call subarticulation_octave_layer_set_event_id
        $ii4 := $subarticulation_event_id18
        $group_count001 := $MARK_1
        call subarticulation_event_set_event_mark
        $group_count001 := $subarticulation_event_id18
        call subarticulation_event_disallow_groups
        $transition_type20 := 0
        while($transition_type20 <= (%subarticulations_dynamic_layers[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count0]] - 1)) 
          $transition_dyn_layer00 := 0
          while($transition_dyn_layer00 <= 5) 
            $group_count001 := $subarticulation_event_id18
            $ii4 := ((((%subarticulations_group_idx[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count0]] + 1) + (((6 * %subarticulations_rr_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count0]]) * %subarticulations_dynamic_layers[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count0]]) * ($i17 * (1 + %subarticulations_release_group[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count0]])))) + ((($rr0 * %subarticulations_dynamic_layers[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count0]]) * (%subarticulations_release_group[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count0]] + 1)) * 6)) + (($transition_type20 * (%subarticulations_release_group[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count0]] + 1)) * 6)) + $transition_dyn_layer00
            call subarticulation_event_allow_groups
            inc($transition_dyn_layer00)
          end while
          inc($transition_type20)
        end while
        $group_count001 := $subarticulation_event_id18
        $ii4 := %_loaded_subarticulations_volume[($_ret660 * 32) + (($purge_state0 * 4) + $subarticulation_id1)] * 1000
        $iii1 := 1
        call subarticulation_event_change_vol
        if((%subarticulations_start_offset[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count0]] > 0) and ($use_constant_delay = 1))
          $group_count000 := $subarticulation_event_id18
          $_ret6600 := %subarticulations_start_offset[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count0]]
          call subarticulation_event_fade_in
        end if
        if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$group_count0]] = 6)
          $iii1 := $subarticulation_event_id18
          $group_count001 := $string0100
          call repetition_engine_add
          if(((($ENGINE_UPTIME + %_repetition_interval_time_humanization[($_ret660 * 4096) + (($purge_state0 * 512) + $subarticulation_id1)]) - $repetition_engine_start_time) mod %_repetition_interval_time[($_ret660 * 4096) + (($purge_state0 * 512) + $subarticulation_id1)]) > 5)
            $group_count001 := $subarticulation_event_id18
            $_ret6600 := 1
            $group_count000 := 0
            call subarticulation_event_fade_out
          end if
        end if
      else
        $string0100 := 0
        $string0200 := 0

function repetition_engine_update_tempo
  ~subarticulation_modulation_strength01 := real(ms_to_ticks(60000000)) / 960.
  if((~subarticulation_modulation_strength01 # ~tempo) or ($NI_CALLBACK_TYPE # $NI_CB_TYPE_LISTENER))
    $fade_in_start01 := 0
    $fade_in_range01 := 0
    $rr10 := 0
    while($rr10 <= 0) 
      $fade_in_start01 := 0
      while($fade_in_start01 <= 7) 
        $fade_in_range01 := 0
        while($fade_in_range01 <= 511) 
          if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($rr10 * 32) + (($fade_in_start01 * 4) + $fade_in_range01)]]] = 6)
            %_repetition_interval_time[($rr10 * 4096) + (($fade_in_start01 * 512) + $fade_in_range01)] := int((60000. / ~subarticulation_modulation_strength01) * (4. / real(%_loaded_subarticulations_repetition_speed[($rr10 * 32) + (($fade_in_start01 * 4) + $fade_in_range01)])))
          end if
          inc($fade_in_range01)
        end while
        inc($fade_in_start01)
      end while
      inc($rr10)
    end while
    ~tempo := ~subarticulation_modulation_strength01
  end if
end function
