            $subarticulation_event1 := $i150
            $idx25 := $idx2300
            call repetition_engine_remove
          end if
        else
          $ii4 := %repetition_engine_subarticulation_events[$result150]
          $subarticulation_event1 := $ii4
          $idx25 := $group_count000
          call repetition_engine_remove
        end if
      end if
      inc($result150)
    end while
    if($result1500 = 1)
      ~subarticulation_modulation_strength01 := ~subarticulation_modulation_strength01
      $rr10 := $result150
      $fade_in_start01 := $ii4
      $fade_in_range01 := $group_count000
      call repetition_engine_update_tempo
      $i := 0
      while(($i < num_elements(%repetition_played_subarticulation_events)) and (%repetition_played_subarticulation_events[$i] # -1)) 
        %_repetition_interval_time_humanization[(%articulation_event_instrument[%subarticulation_event_articulation_event[%repetition_played_subarticulation_events[$i]]] * 4096) + ((%articulation_event_keyswitch[%subarticulation_event_articulation_event[%repetition_played_subarticulation_events[$i]]] * 512) + %subarticulation_event_subarticulation_idx[%repetition_played_subarticulation_events[$i]])] := random(- %_articulation_humanization[(%articulation_event_instrument[%subarticulation_event_articulation_event[%repetition_played_subarticulation_events[$i]]] * 8) + %articulation_event_keyswitch[%subarticulation_event_articulation_event[%repetition_played_subarticulation_events[$i]]]] / 2, %_articulation_humanization[(%articulation_event_instrument[%subarticulation_event_articulation_event[%repetition_played_subarticulation_events[$i]]] * 8) + %articulation_event_keyswitch[%subarticulation_event_articulation_event[%repetition_played_subarticulation_events[$i]]]] / 2)
        inc($i)
      end while
    end if
    if($i1200 = 0)
      $repetition_engine_active := 0
      $repetition_engine_start_time := -1
    end if
  end if
end function
function update_dynamic_range_cursor
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_cursor), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 5) + int((real((($group_count001 * (1 + (sh_right(127 - $group_count001, 31) .or. sh_right($group_count001 - 1, 31)))) - sh_right($group_count001 - 1, 31)) - (127 * sh_right(127 - $group_count001, 31))) / 127.) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))))
end function
function update_circle_modwheel_position
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_center_circle_indicator), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, $subarticulation_event1 - 1)
end function
function update_modwheel_assignment_cursor
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_cursor), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 5) + int(real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)) * (real($subarticulation_event1) / 127.)))
end function
function update_keyswitch_volume_curve_cursor
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_cursor), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 5) + int(real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)) * (real($subarticulation_event1) / 127.)))
end function
function editor_update_modwheel_position
  $group_count001 := $group_count001
  call update_dynamic_range_cursor
  $subarticulation_event1 := $group_count001
  call update_circle_modwheel_position
  $subarticulation_event1 := $group_count001
  call update_modwheel_assignment_cursor
  $subarticulation_event1 := $group_count001
  call update_keyswitch_volume_curve_cursor
end function
function subarticulation_group_count
  $transition_note_event00 := 0
  if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id0]] = 2)
    $transition_note_event00 := 6 * ((%subarticulations_dynamic_layers[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id0]] * 3) + %subarticulations_trans_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id0]])
  else
    $transition_note_event00 := (6 * %subarticulations_interval_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id0]]) * ((%subarticulations_rr_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id0]] * %subarticulations_dynamic_layers[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id0]]) * (1 + %subarticulations_release_group[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id0]]))
  end if
  $ret14 := $transition_note_event00
end function
function subarticulation_browser_load_category
  $subarticulation_event1 := 0
  while($subarticulation_event1 <= (num_elements(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection) - 1)) 
    set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    if(%_subarticulation_browser_entries[($idx25 * 14) + $subarticulation_event1] # -1)
      set_control_par_str(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !subarticulations_full_name[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_subarticulation_browser_entries[($idx25 * 14) + $subarticulation_event1]]])
      if(%_subarticulation_browser_entries[($idx25 * 14) + $subarticulation_event1] = %_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
        set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
      else
        set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
      end if
      set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    end if
    inc($subarticulation_event1)
  end while
  $subarticulation_event1 := 0
  while($subarticulation_event1 <= (num_elements(%btn_subarticulation_browser_category) - 1)) 
    if($subarticulation_event1 = $idx25)
      set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_category[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
    else
      set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_category[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
    end if
    inc($subarticulation_event1)
  end while
  $subarticulation_browser_active_category := $idx25
end function
function move_legato_buffer_to_instrument
  $idx25 := 0
  $fade_out_range01 := 0
  $ii4 := 0
  while($ii4 <= 1) 
    $idx25 := 0
    while($idx25 <= 127) 
      $fade_out_range01 := 0
      while($fade_out_range01 <= 24) 
        %_legato_data_sus_fade_in_time[($result1500 * 204800) + (($i1200 * 25600) + (($result150 * 6400) + (($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time[($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01)]
        %_legato_data_sus_release_time[($result1500 * 204800) + (($i1200 * 25600) + (($result150 * 6400) + (($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time[($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01)]
        %_legato_data_sus_wait_time[($result1500 * 204800) + (($i1200 * 25600) + (($result150 * 6400) + (($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time[($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01)]
        %_legato_data_trans_fade_in_time[($result1500 * 204800) + (($i1200 * 25600) + (($result150 * 6400) + (($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_in_time[($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01)]
        %_legato_data_trans_fade_out_time[($result1500 * 204800) + (($i1200 * 25600) + (($result150 * 6400) + (($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time[($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01)]
        %_legato_data_trans_zone_start[($result1500 * 204800) + (($i1200 * 25600) + (($result150 * 6400) + (($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_start[($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01)]
        %_legato_data_trans_zone_volume[($result1500 * 204800) + (($i1200 * 25600) + (($result150 * 6400) + (($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_volume[($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01)]
        %_legato_data_sus_fade_in_time_offset[($result1500 * 204800) + (($i1200 * 25600) + (($result150 * 6400) + (($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time_offset[($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01)]
        %_legato_data_sus_release_time_offset[($result1500 * 204800) + (($i1200 * 25600) + (($result150 * 6400) + (($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time_offset[($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01)]
        %_legato_data_sus_wait_time_offset[($result1500 * 204800) + (($i1200 * 25600) + (($result150 * 6400) + (($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time_offset[($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01)]
        %_legato_data_trans_fade_in_time_offset[($result1500 * 204800) + (($i1200 * 25600) + (($result150 * 6400) + (($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_in_time_offset[($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01)]
        %_legato_data_trans_fade_out_time_offset[($result1500 * 204800) + (($i1200 * 25600) + (($result150 * 6400) + (($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time_offset[($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01)]
        %_legato_data_trans_zone_start_offset[($result1500 * 204800) + (($i1200 * 25600) + (($result150 * 6400) + (($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_start_offset[($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01)]
        %_legato_data_trans_zone_volume_offset[($result1500 * 204800) + (($i1200 * 25600) + (($result150 * 6400) + (($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_volume_offset[($ii4 * 3200) + (($idx25 * 25) + $fade_out_range01)]
        inc($fade_out_range01)
      end while
      inc($idx25)
    end while
    inc($ii4)
  end while
end function
function editor_page_open
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_editor_page), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_articulation_humanize), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_humanization[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_articulation_humanize), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_articulation_humanize & " ms")
  if(%_articulation_release[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch] >= 0)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_articulation_release), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_release[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_articulation_release), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_articulation_release & " ms")
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_articulation_release_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    $btn_articulation_release := 0
  else
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_articulation_release), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "")
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_articulation_release_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    $btn_articulation_release := 1
  end if
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_min), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_max), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch] * -1)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope) - 1)) 
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, int(round(real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) + (real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.) - int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) * pow(real($i) / real(num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope)), (real(%_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 100.) + 1.)))))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) - get_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
    inc($i)
  end while
  $subarticulation_event1 := $idx25
  $group_count001 := $selected_subarticulation
  $group_count000 := $idx25
  $idx25 := 0
  while($idx25 <= (num_elements(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection) - 1)) 
    if($idx25 # $group_count001)
      set_control_par(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[$idx25], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
    else
      set_control_par(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[$idx25], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
    end if
    inc($idx25)
  end while
  if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] # -1)
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_title), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "    " & !subarticulations_full_name[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]])
  else
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_title), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "    Empty")
  end if
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_solo_subarticulation), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_subarticulations_solo_states[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulations_volume[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_volume & " dB")
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_subarticulation_repetition_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_repetition_speed_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_subarticulation_rr_mode), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_rr_mode_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  if(((%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 0) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 5)) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 6))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulations_tightness[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_tightness & " %")
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    $mnu_subarticulation_rr_mode := %_loaded_subarticulations_rr_mode[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_subarticulation_rr_mode), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_rr_mode_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  end if
  if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 6)
    $mnu_subarticulation_repetition_speed := %_loaded_subarticulations_repetition_speed[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_subarticulation_repetition_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_repetition_speed_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  end if
  if(((%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 1) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 2)) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 4))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulations_vibrato[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_vibrato & " %")
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  end if
  if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 2)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulations_trans_volume[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_trans_volume & " dB")
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulation_trans_speed[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_trans_speed & " %")
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    $btn_subarticulation_trans_speed := %_loaded_subarticulation_trans_speed_auto[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    if($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed = 1)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    end if
  end if
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 3) 
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)] # -1)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      if($i = $selected_subarticulation)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-selected-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-left-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-right-" & $i)
      else
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-unselected-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-left-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-right-" & $i)
      end if
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, 127 - %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] + %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] - %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(-200. + ((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(round((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  ?xy_dynamic_range[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_dynamic_range[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[0] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
  $group_count001 := %modulation_positions[0]
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_cursor), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 5) + int((real((($group_count001 * (1 + (sh_right(127 - $group_count001, 31) .or. sh_right($group_count001 - 1, 31)))) - sh_right($group_count001 - 1, 31)) - (127 * sh_right(127 - $group_count001, 31))) / 127.) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))))
  @txt_keyswitch_name := !_articulation_names[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_min), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_max), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch] * -1)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope) - 1)) 
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, int(round(real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) + (real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.) - int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) * pow(real($i) / real(num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope)), (real(%_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 100.) + 1.)))))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) - get_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 3) 
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)] # -1)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      if($i = $selected_subarticulation)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-selected-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-left-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-right-" & $i)
      else
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-unselected-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-left-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-right-" & $i)
      end if
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, 127 - %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] + %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] - %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(-200. + ((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(round((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  ?xy_dynamic_range[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_dynamic_range[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[0] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
  $group_count001 := %modulation_positions[0]
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_cursor), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 5) + int((real((($group_count001 * (1 + (sh_right(127 - $group_count001, 31) .or. sh_right($group_count001 - 1, 31)))) - sh_right($group_count001 - 1, 31)) - (127 * sh_right(127 - $group_count001, 31))) / 127.) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))))
end function

  set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_main_page), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
end function

  set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_editor_page), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
end function
function mixer_page_close
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_mixer_page), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
end function
function show_keyswitches
  if($fade_out_end01 = 1)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_keyswitches), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  else
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_keyswitches), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  end if
end function
function authoring_close
  $btn_show_authoring_tools := 0
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_authoring), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  $authoring_page_active := 0
end function
function main_page_close
  call authoring_close
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_main_page), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
end function

  set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_mixer_page), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
end function

function settings_open
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_settings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_settings), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
end function
function settings_close
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_settings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_settings), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
end function
function find_loaded_legato
  $authoring_page_active := 0
  if(%_loaded_subarticulations[0] # -1)
    if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[0]]] = 2)
      $authoring_page_active := 1
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_authoring_legato_title), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !subarticulations_full_name[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[0]]] & " (" & %_loaded_subarticulations[0] & ")")
    end if
  end if
end function
function authoring_open
  call find_loaded_legato
  $idx25 := 60
  $subarticulation_event1 := 60
  $iii1 := 0
  call update_authoring_transition
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_authoring), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
end function
function update_subarticulation_selection
  $group_count001 := $selected_subarticulation
  $group_count000 := $idx25
  $idx25 := 0
  while($idx25 <= (num_elements(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection) - 1)) 
    if($idx25 # $group_count001)
      set_control_par(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[$idx25], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
    else
      set_control_par(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[$idx25], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
    end if
    inc($idx25)
  end while
  if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] # -1)
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_title), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "    " & !subarticulations_full_name[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]])
  else
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_title), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "    Empty")
  end if
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_solo_subarticulation), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_subarticulations_solo_states[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulations_volume[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_volume & " dB")
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_subarticulation_repetition_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_repetition_speed_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_subarticulation_rr_mode), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_rr_mode_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  if(((%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 0) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 5)) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 6))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulations_tightness[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_tightness & " %")
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    $mnu_subarticulation_rr_mode := %_loaded_subarticulations_rr_mode[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_subarticulation_rr_mode), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_rr_mode_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  end if
  if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 6)
    $mnu_subarticulation_repetition_speed := %_loaded_subarticulations_repetition_speed[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_subarticulation_repetition_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_repetition_speed_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  end if
  if(((%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 1) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 2)) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 4))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulations_vibrato[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_vibrato & " %")
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  end if
  if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 2)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulations_trans_volume[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_trans_volume & " dB")
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulation_trans_speed[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_trans_speed & " %")
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    $btn_subarticulation_trans_speed := %_loaded_subarticulation_trans_speed_auto[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    if($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed = 1)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    end if
  end if
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 3) 
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)] # -1)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      if($i = $selected_subarticulation)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-selected-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-left-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-right-" & $i)
      else
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-unselected-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-left-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-right-" & $i)
      end if
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, 127 - %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] + %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] - %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(-200. + ((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(round((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  ?xy_dynamic_range[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_dynamic_range[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[0] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
  $group_count001 := %modulation_positions[0]
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_cursor), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 5) + int((real((($group_count001 * (1 + (sh_right(127 - $group_count001, 31) .or. sh_right($group_count001 - 1, 31)))) - sh_right($group_count001 - 1, 31)) - (127 * sh_right(127 - $group_count001, 31))) / 127.) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))))
end function
function subarticulation_browser_open
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_subarticulation_browser), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] # -1)
    $idx25 := %type_to_category[%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]]]
    $subarticulation_event1 := 0
    while($subarticulation_event1 <= (num_elements(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection) - 1)) 
      set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      if(%_subarticulation_browser_entries[($idx25 * 14) + $subarticulation_event1] # -1)
        set_control_par_str(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !subarticulations_full_name[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_subarticulation_browser_entries[($idx25 * 14) + $subarticulation_event1]]])
        if(%_subarticulation_browser_entries[($idx25 * 14) + $subarticulation_event1] = %_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
          set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
        else
          set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
        end if
        set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      end if
      inc($subarticulation_event1)
    end while
    $subarticulation_event1 := 0
    while($subarticulation_event1 <= (num_elements(%btn_subarticulation_browser_category) - 1)) 
      if($subarticulation_event1 = $idx25)
        set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_category[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
      else
        set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_category[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
      end if
      inc($subarticulation_event1)
    end while
    $subarticulation_browser_active_category := $idx25
  end if
end function
function subarticulation_browser_close
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_subarticulation_browser), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_title), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
end function
function update_keyswitch_volume_curve
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_min), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_max), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch] * -1)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope) - 1)) 
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, int(round(real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) + (real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.) - int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) * pow(real($i) / real(num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope)), (real(%_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 100.) + 1.)))))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) - get_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function update_modwheel_assignment_control
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] + %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] - %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(-200. + ((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(round((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
end function
function update_modwheel_assignment_circles
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 3) 
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)] # -1)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      if($i = $selected_subarticulation)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-selected-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-left-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-right-" & $i)
      else
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-unselected-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-left-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-right-" & $i)
      end if
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, 127 - %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function update_dynamic_range_control
  ?xy_dynamic_range[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_dynamic_range[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[0] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
  $group_count001 := %modulation_positions[0]
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_cursor), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 5) + int((real((($group_count001 * (1 + (sh_right(127 - $group_count001, 31) .or. sh_right($group_count001 - 1, 31)))) - sh_right($group_count001 - 1, 31)) - (127 * sh_right(127 - $group_count001, 31))) / 127.) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))))
end function
function angle_to_value
  ~angle1 := ~dy0 + (~NI_MATH_PI / 2.)
  if(~angle1 > (~NI_MATH_PI * 2.))
    ~angle1 := ~angle1 - (2. * ~NI_MATH_PI)
  end if
  ~angle1 := abs(~angle1 - (2. * ~NI_MATH_PI))
  $group_count001 := int((127. * (~angle1 - ~subarticulation_modulation_strength01)) / (~transition_speed0 - ~subarticulation_modulation_strength01))
end function
function move_to_legato_buffer
  $i1200 := 0
  $result1500 := 0
  $result150 := 0
  while($result150 <= 1) 
    $i1200 := 0
    while($i1200 <= 127) 
      $result1500 := 0
      while($result1500 <= 24) 
        %_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time[($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500)] := %_legato_data_sus_fade_in_time[($group_count000 * 204800) + (($string02 * 25600) + (($ii4 * 6400) + (($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time[($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500)] := %_legato_data_sus_release_time[($group_count000 * 204800) + (($string02 * 25600) + (($ii4 * 6400) + (($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time[($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500)] := %_legato_data_sus_wait_time[($group_count000 * 204800) + (($string02 * 25600) + (($ii4 * 6400) + (($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_in_time[($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500)] := %_legato_data_trans_fade_in_time[($group_count000 * 204800) + (($string02 * 25600) + (($ii4 * 6400) + (($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time[($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500)] := %_legato_data_trans_fade_out_time[($group_count000 * 204800) + (($string02 * 25600) + (($ii4 * 6400) + (($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_start[($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500)] := %_legato_data_trans_zone_start[($group_count000 * 204800) + (($string02 * 25600) + (($ii4 * 6400) + (($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_volume[($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500)] := %_legato_data_trans_zone_volume[($group_count000 * 204800) + (($string02 * 25600) + (($ii4 * 6400) + (($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time_offset[($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500)] := %_legato_data_sus_fade_in_time_offset[($group_count000 * 204800) + (($string02 * 25600) + (($ii4 * 6400) + (($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time_offset[($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500)] := %_legato_data_sus_release_time_offset[($group_count000 * 204800) + (($string02 * 25600) + (($ii4 * 6400) + (($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time_offset[($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500)] := %_legato_data_sus_wait_time_offset[($group_count000 * 204800) + (($string02 * 25600) + (($ii4 * 6400) + (($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_in_time_offset[($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500)] := %_legato_data_trans_fade_in_time_offset[($group_count000 * 204800) + (($string02 * 25600) + (($ii4 * 6400) + (($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time_offset[($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500)] := %_legato_data_trans_fade_out_time_offset[($group_count000 * 204800) + (($string02 * 25600) + (($ii4 * 6400) + (($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_start_offset[($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500)] := %_legato_data_trans_zone_start_offset[($group_count000 * 204800) + (($string02 * 25600) + (($ii4 * 6400) + (($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_volume_offset[($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500)] := %_legato_data_trans_zone_volume_offset[($group_count000 * 204800) + (($string02 * 25600) + (($ii4 * 6400) + (($result150 * 3200) + (($i1200 * 25) + $result1500))))]
        inc($result1500)
      end while
      inc($i1200)
    end while
    inc($result150)
  end while
end function
on persistence_changed
  $idx25 := %CC[1]
  call set_background_animation
  call set_key_colors
  call keyswitches_color_keys
end on
on note
  ignore_event($EVENT_ID)
  set_key_pressed($EVENT_NOTE, 1)
  $transition_note_event00 := $EVENT_NOTE
  call keyswitches_on_note
  if(%pressed_keys[$EVENT_NOTE] = -1)
    %pressed_keys[$EVENT_NOTE] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
    %last_pressed[$EVENT_NOTE] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
    %key_velocity[$EVENT_NOTE] := $EVENT_VELOCITY
    inc($num_pressed_keys)
  end if
  $last_on_note_callback := $NI_CALLBACK_ID
  %wait_time0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] := $note_selection_time * 1000
  call wait_or_zero
  if($last_on_note_callback = $NI_CALLBACK_ID)
    call update_selected_notes
  end if
end on
on release
  if(get_event_mark($EVENT_ID, $MARK_1) = 0)
    set_key_pressed($EVENT_NOTE, 0)
    $last_release_callback := $NI_CALLBACK_ID
    ignore_event($EVENT_ID)
    %pressed_keys[$EVENT_NOTE] := -1
    dec($num_pressed_keys)
    if($sustain_pedal = 0)
      $i130 := 0
      $event10 := $EVENT_NOTE
      call articulations_note_off
      %wait_time0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] := $note_selection_time * 1000
      call wait_or_zero
      $i := 0
      while($i <= 0) 
        %_pressed_notes_per_instrument[($i * 128) + $EVENT_NOTE] := 0
        inc($i)
      end while
      if($last_release_callback = $NI_CALLBACK_ID)
        call update_selected_notes
      end if
    end if
  end if
end on
on controller
  ignore_controller
  %controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] := %CC[$CC_NUM]
  if($CC_NUM = 1)
    $idx25 := %CC[1]
    call buffer_modwheel_animation
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_modwheel_slider), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %CC[1])
  end if
  if($CC_NUM = 64)
    if(%CC[64] > 63)
      $sustain_pedal_actual := 1
    else
      $sustain_pedal_actual := 0
      $sustain_pedal := 0
      $i := 0
      while($i <= 127) 
        if(%pressed_keys[$i] = -1)
          $ii := 0
          while($ii <= 0) 
            $i130 := $ii
            $event10 := $i
            call articulations_note_off
            inc($ii)
          end while
        end if
        inc($i)
      end while
    end if
  end if
  %wait_time0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] := ($lookahead * 1000) * $use_constant_delay
  call wait_or_zero
  $sustain_pedal := $sustain_pedal_actual
  if($CC_NUM = 1)
    $string0200 := 0
    $string0100 := %controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100]
    call set_modulation_position
    call cc_on_controller
  end if
end on
on poly_at
  $string0200 := $POLY_AT_NUM
  $string0100 := %POLY_AT[$POLY_AT_NUM]
  call set_modulation_position
  call cc_on_controller
end on
on listener
  call delay_buffer_execute
  $next_free_idx0000 := $next_free_idx0000
  $i4000 := $i4000
  call repetition_engine_listener
  if(($animation_frame_counter = 0) and ($next_modwheel_animation_frame # -1))
    $idx25 := $next_modwheel_animation_frame

    if(get_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_editor_page), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE) = $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)

    end if

  end if
  $animation_frame_counter := ($animation_frame_counter + 1) mod 4
end on

  %wait_time0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] := $NI_UI_ID

        wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_in_time_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & !legato_name0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] & "_sus_trans_fade_in_time_offset.nka"))
        wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & !legato_name0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] & "_sus_trans_fade_out_time_offset.nka"))
        wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_start_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & !legato_name0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] & "_sus_trans_zone_start_offset.nka"))
        wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_volume_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & !legato_name0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] & "_sus_trans_zone_volume_offset.nka"))
        $result1500 := $selected_instrument
        $i1200 := $selected_keyswitch
        $result150 := $selected_subarticulation
        $ii4 := $subarticulation_event1
        $string02 := $idx25
        $group_count000 := $fade_out_range01
        call move_legato_buffer_to_instrument
      end if
      $idx25 := $subarticulation_browser_active_category
      $subarticulation_event1 := $subarticulation_event1
      call subarticulation_browser_load_category
      $idx25 := $subarticulation_event1
      call editor_page_open
    end if
  end if
end on

on ui_control(?xy_modwheel_assignment)
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[1] := 1.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[5] := 1.
  if($NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE = $NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_LEFT_BUTTON_DOWN)
    if((get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX) = 0) or (get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX) = 4))
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_fade_circle_md), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    end if
  else
    if($NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE = $NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_LEFT_BUTTON_UP)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_fade_circle_md), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    end if
  end if
  $ma_cb_id := $NI_CALLBACK_ID
  if((get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX) = 2) and (?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] <= ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]))
    if(?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] < ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2])
      ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] := ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]
    end if
    %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] * 127.)
  else
    if(((get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX) = 0) and (?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] <= ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0])) and (?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] <= ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]))
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_fade_circle_md), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) - 20)))
      %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := int(round((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * 127.))
    else
      if(((get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX) = 4) and (?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] <= ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4])) and (?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] <= ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6]))
        set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_fade_circle_md), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) - 20)))
        %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]) * 127.)
      else
        if((get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX) = 6) and (?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] <= ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6]))
          if(?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] > ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6])
            ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] := ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6]
          end if
          %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] * 127.)
        end if
      end if
    end if
  end if
  wait(10000)
  if($ma_cb_id = $NI_CALLBACK_ID)
    call update_modwheel_assignment_control
    call update_modwheel_assignment_circles
  end if
end on
on ui_control(?xy_dynamic_range)
  $dr_cb_id := $NI_CALLBACK_ID
  if((get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_dynamic_range), $CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX) = 0) and (?xy_dynamic_range[0] <= ?xy_dynamic_range[2]))
    %_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := int(?xy_dynamic_range[0] * 127.)

    end if
  end if
  wait(10000)

    call update_dynamic_range_control
  end if
end on
