on ui_control(?xy_center_circles)
  $cc_cb_id := $NI_CALLBACK_ID
  if($NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE = $NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_LEFT_BUTTON_DOWN)
    ~transition_speed0 := ?xy_center_circles[0] - 0.5
    ~subarticulation_modulation_strength01 := sqrt((~transition_speed0 * ~transition_speed0) + (~dy0 * ~dy0))
    ?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] := ~subarticulation_modulation_strength01
    ~subarticulation_modulation_strength01 := ?xy_center_circles[0] - 0.5
    ~dy0 := ?xy_center_circles[1] - 0.5
    ~cos_theta0 := ~subarticulation_modulation_strength01 / sqrt((~subarticulation_modulation_strength01 * ~subarticulation_modulation_strength01) + (~dy0 * ~dy0))
    ~angle1 := acos(~cos_theta0)
    if(~dy0 < 0.)
      ~angle1 := (2. * ~NI_MATH_PI) - ~angle1
    end if
    ~transition_speed0 := ~angle1
    ?angle2[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] := ~transition_speed0
    ~dy0 := ?angle2[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100]
    ~subarticulation_modulation_strength01 := 0.7
    ~transition_speed0 := (~NI_MATH_PI * 2.) - 0.7
    call angle_to_value
    %controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] := $group_count001
    if((?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] >= 0.32) and (?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] < 0.36))
      $selected_subarticulation := 0
    else
      if((?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] >= 0.36) and (?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] < 0.4))
        $selected_subarticulation := 1
      else
        if((?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] >= 0.4) and (?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] < 0.44))
          $selected_subarticulation := 2
        else
          if((?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] >= 0.44) and (?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] < 0.48))
            $selected_subarticulation := 3
          end if
        end if
      end if
    end if
    if(abs(%controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] - %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) < 10)
      $selected_circle_end := 0
    else
      if(abs(%controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] - %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) < 10)
        $selected_circle_end := 1
      else
        $selected_circle_end := -1
      end if
    end if
    call update_subarticulation_selection
  end if
  if($NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE = $NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_DRAG)
    wait(10000)
    if(($cc_cb_id = $NI_CALLBACK_ID) and ($selected_circle_end # -1))
      ~subarticulation_modulation_strength01 := ?xy_center_circles[0] - 0.5
      ~dy0 := ?xy_center_circles[1] - 0.5
      ~cos_theta0 := ~subarticulation_modulation_strength01 / sqrt((~subarticulation_modulation_strength01 * ~subarticulation_modulation_strength01) + (~dy0 * ~dy0))
      ~angle1 := acos(~cos_theta0)
      if(~dy0 < 0.)
        ~angle1 := (2. * ~NI_MATH_PI) - ~angle1
      end if
      ~transition_speed0 := ~angle1
      ?angle2[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] := ~transition_speed0
      ~dy0 := ?angle2[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100]
      ~subarticulation_modulation_strength01 := 0.7
      ~transition_speed0 := (~NI_MATH_PI * 2.) - 0.7
      call angle_to_value
      %controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] := $group_count001
      if($selected_circle_end = 0)
        if(%controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] < ((%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] - %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) - %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]))
          %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := %controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100]
        end if
      else
        if($selected_circle_end = 1)
          if(%controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] > ((%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] + %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) + %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]))
            %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := %controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100]
          end if
        end if
      end if
      call update_modwheel_assignment_control
      call update_modwheel_assignment_circles
    end if
  end if
end on
on ui_control($mnu_mixer_bleed_channel)
  $group_count001 := %btn_mixer_channel_enable[4]
  $subarticulation_event1 := search(%sli_mixer_channel_volume, $group_count001)
  if($subarticulation_event1 # -1)
    set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_VOLUME, get_control_par(%sli_mixer_channel_volume[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE), -1, -1, $NI_BUS_OFFSET + $subarticulation_event1)
    if($subarticulation_event1 = 4)
      set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_VOLUME, get_control_par(%sli_mixer_channel_volume[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE), -1, -1, $NI_BUS_OFFSET + 5)
    end if
  end if
  $subarticulation_event1 := search(%btn_mixer_channel_enable, $group_count001)
  if($subarticulation_event1 # -1)
    if($subarticulation_event1 < 4)
      %microphone_position_states[$subarticulation_event1] := get_control_par(%btn_mixer_channel_enable[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
    else
      %microphone_position_states[$subarticulation_event1 + $mnu_mixer_bleed_channel] := get_control_par(%btn_mixer_channel_enable[$subarticulation_event1], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
      %microphone_position_states[$subarticulation_event1 + (1 - $mnu_mixer_bleed_channel)] := 0
    end if
    $i17 := $idx25
    $ii4 := $iii1
    $iii1 := $fade_in_range01
    $group_count000 := $rr10
    $group_count001 := $fade_out_end01
    $fade_in_range01 := 0
    $idx25 := 0
    $_iter0 := 0
    while($_iter0 <= (num_elements(%subarticulation_is_loaded0) - 1)) 
      %subarticulation_is_loaded0[$_iter0] := 0
      inc($_iter0)
    end while
    $idx25 := 0
    while($idx25 <= 0) 
      $fade_in_range01 := 0
      while($fade_in_range01 <= 7) 
        $idx25 := 0
        while($idx25 <= 3) 
          if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($idx25 * 32) + (($fade_in_range01 * 4) + $idx25)] # -1)
            %subarticulation_is_loaded0[%_loaded_subarticulations[($idx25 * 32) + (($fade_in_range01 * 4) + $idx25)]] := %subarticulation_is_loaded0[%_loaded_subarticulations[($idx25 * 32) + (($fade_in_range01 * 4) + $idx25)]] + %_keyswitch_purge_states[($idx25 * 8) + $fade_in_range01]
          end if
          inc($idx25)
        end while
        inc($fade_in_range01)
      end while
      inc($idx25)
    end while
    $idx25 := 0
    while($idx25 <= 511) 
      if(%subarticulations_group_idx[$idx25] # $NI_NOT_FOUND)
        if(%subarticulation_is_loaded0[$idx25] = 0)
          $subarticulation_id1 := $idx25
          $purge_state0 := 0
          $group_count00 := $fade_out_range01
          $i := 0
          $subarticulation_id0 := $subarticulation_id1
          $group_count0 := $transition_note_event00
          call subarticulation_group_count
          $subarticulation_event1 := $ret14
          while($i <= ($subarticulation_event1 - 1)) 
            purge_group((%subarticulations_group_idx[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id1]] + $i) + 1, $purge_state0 * %microphone_position_states[$i mod 6])
            inc($i)
            $subarticulation_id0 := $subarticulation_id1
            $group_count0 := $transition_note_event00
            call subarticulation_group_count
            $subarticulation_event1 := $ret14
          end while
          $subarticulation_event1 := $_ret660
        end if
      end if
      inc($idx25)
    end while
    $idx25 := 0
    while($idx25 <= 511) 
      if(%subarticulations_group_idx[$idx25] # $NI_NOT_FOUND)
        if(%subarticulation_is_loaded0[$idx25] > 0)
          $subarticulation_id1 := $idx25
          $purge_state0 := 1
          $group_count00 := $transition_note_event00
          $i := 0
          $subarticulation_id0 := $subarticulation_id1
          $group_count0 := $transition_note_event00
          call subarticulation_group_count
          $subarticulation_event1 := $ret14
          while($i <= ($subarticulation_event1 - 1)) 
            purge_group((%subarticulations_group_idx[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id1]] + $i) + 1, $purge_state0 * %microphone_position_states[$i mod 6])
            inc($i)
            $subarticulation_id0 := $subarticulation_id1
            $group_count0 := $transition_note_event00
            call subarticulation_group_count
            $subarticulation_event1 := $ret14
          end while
          $fade_out_range01 := $_ret660
        end if
      end if
      inc($idx25)
    end while
    $fade_in_start01 := $_ret6600
  end if
  attach_level_meter(%lvl_mixer_channel_volume[8], -1, -1, 0, 4 + $mnu_mixer_bleed_channel)
  attach_level_meter(%lvl_mixer_channel_volume[9], -1, -1, 1, 4 + $mnu_mixer_bleed_channel)
end on
on ui_control($btn_unpurge_all)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(%microphone_position_states) - 1)) 
    %microphone_position_states[$i] := 1
    inc($i)
  end while
  $fade_in_range01 := 0
  $idx25 := 0
  $_iter0 := 0
  while($_iter0 <= (num_elements(%subarticulation_is_loaded0) - 1)) 
    %subarticulation_is_loaded0[$_iter0] := 0
    inc($_iter0)
  end while
  $idx25 := 0
  while($idx25 <= 0) 
    $fade_in_range01 := 0
    while($fade_in_range01 <= 7) 
      $idx25 := 0
      while($idx25 <= 3) 
        if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($idx25 * 32) + (($fade_in_range01 * 4) + $idx25)] # -1)
          %subarticulation_is_loaded0[%_loaded_subarticulations[($idx25 * 32) + (($fade_in_range01 * 4) + $idx25)]] := %subarticulation_is_loaded0[%_loaded_subarticulations[($idx25 * 32) + (($fade_in_range01 * 4) + $idx25)]] + %_keyswitch_purge_states[($idx25 * 8) + $fade_in_range01]
        end if
        inc($idx25)
      end while
      inc($fade_in_range01)
    end while
    inc($idx25)
  end while
  $idx25 := 0
  while($idx25 <= 511) 
    if(%subarticulations_group_idx[$idx25] # $NI_NOT_FOUND)
      if(%subarticulation_is_loaded0[$idx25] = 0)
        $subarticulation_id1 := $idx25
        $purge_state0 := 0
        $group_count00 := $fade_out_range01
        $i := 0
        $subarticulation_id0 := $subarticulation_id1
        $group_count0 := $transition_note_event00
        call subarticulation_group_count
        $subarticulation_event1 := $ret14
        while($i <= ($subarticulation_event1 - 1)) 
          purge_group((%subarticulations_group_idx[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id1]] + $i) + 1, $purge_state0 * %microphone_position_states[$i mod 6])
          inc($i)
          $subarticulation_id0 := $subarticulation_id1
          $group_count0 := $transition_note_event00
          call subarticulation_group_count
          $subarticulation_event1 := $ret14
        end while
        $subarticulation_event1 := $_ret660
      end if
    end if
    inc($idx25)
  end while
  $idx25 := 0
  while($idx25 <= 511) 
    if(%subarticulations_group_idx[$idx25] # $NI_NOT_FOUND)
      if(%subarticulation_is_loaded0[$idx25] > 0)
        $subarticulation_id1 := $idx25
        $purge_state0 := 1
        $group_count00 := $transition_note_event00
        $i := 0
        $subarticulation_id0 := $subarticulation_id1
        $group_count0 := $transition_note_event00
        call subarticulation_group_count
        $subarticulation_event1 := $ret14
        while($i <= ($subarticulation_event1 - 1)) 
          purge_group((%subarticulations_group_idx[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id1]] + $i) + 1, $purge_state0 * %microphone_position_states[$i mod 6])
          inc($i)
          $subarticulation_id0 := $subarticulation_id1
          $group_count0 := $transition_note_event00
          call subarticulation_group_count
          $subarticulation_event1 := $ret14
        end while
        $fade_out_range01 := $_ret660
      end if
    end if
    inc($idx25)
  end while
  $end_note200 := $end_note200
end on

on ui_control($btn_factory_reset)
  $offset100 := 0
  $end_note200 := 0
  $i110000 := 0
  while($i110000 <= 0) 
    %octave_layer[$i110000] := 0
    %octave_shift[$i110000] := 0
    $offset100 := 0
    while($offset100 <= 7) 
      !_articulation_names[($i110000 * 8) + $offset100] := "Empty"
      %_articulation_volume_min[($i110000 * 8) + $offset100] := 0
      %_articulation_volume_max[($i110000 * 8) + $offset100] := 127
      %_articulation_volume_curve[($i110000 * 8) + $offset100] := 0
      %_articulation_humanization[($i110000 * 8) + $offset100] := 0
      %_articulation_release[($i110000 * 8) + $offset100] := -1
      $end_note200 := 0
      while($end_note200 <= 3) 
        %_loaded_subarticulations[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := -1
        %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 0
        %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 127
        %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 0
        %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 0
        %_loaded_subarticulations_volume[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 0
        %_loaded_subarticulations_tightness[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 0
        %_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 0
        %_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 127
        %_loaded_subarticulations_vibrato[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 0
        %_loaded_subarticulations_repetition_speed[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 0
        %_loaded_subarticulations_trans_volume[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 0
        %_loaded_subarticulation_trans_speed[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 0
        %_loaded_subarticulation_trans_speed_auto[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 1
        inc($end_note200)
      end while
      inc($offset100)
    end while
    inc($i110000)
  end while
end on

  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_sustain_wait), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, int((real($sli_sustain_wait) / 1000000.) * 500.) & " + " & int((real($sli_sustain_wait_offset) / 1000000.) * 500.) & " ms")
end on
on ui_control($sli_sustain_fadeIn)
  if(get_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_authoring_edit_all), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) = 1)
    $i := 0
    while($i <= 6399) 
      %_legato_data_sus_fade_in_time[$i] := $sli_sustain_fadeIn
      inc($i)
    end while
  else
    %_legato_data_sus_fade_in_time[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($vlue_authoring_start_note * 25) + (abs($vlue_authoring_end_note - $vlue_authoring_start_note) + (- sh_right(- ($vlue_authoring_end_note - $vlue_authoring_start_note), 31) * 12)))] := $sli_sustain_fadeIn
  end if
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_sustain_fadeIn), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, int((real($sli_sustain_fadeIn) / 1000000.) * 1500.) & " + " & int((real($sli_sustain_fadeIn_offset) / 1000000.) * 1500.) & " ms")
end on
on ui_control($sli_sustain_fadeIn_offset)
  $sli_sustain_fadeIn_offset := (($sli_sustain_fadeIn_offset * (1 + (sh_right((get_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_sustain_fadeIn), $CONTROL_PAR_MAX_VALUE) - $sli_sustain_fadeIn) - $sli_sustain_fadeIn_offset, 31) .or. sh_right($sli_sustain_fadeIn_offset - - $sli_sustain_fadeIn, 31)))) - (- $sli_sustain_fadeIn * sh_right($sli_sustain_fadeIn_offset - - $sli_sustain_fadeIn, 31))) - ((get_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_sustain_fadeIn), $CONTROL_PAR_MAX_VALUE) - $sli_sustain_fadeIn) * sh_right((get_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_sustain_fadeIn), $CONTROL_PAR_MAX_VALUE) - $sli_sustain_fadeIn) - $sli_sustain_fadeIn_offset, 31))
  if(get_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_authoring_edit_all), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) = 1)
    $i := 0
    while($i <= 6399) 
      %_legato_data_sus_fade_in_time_offset[$i] := $sli_sustain_fadeIn_offset
      inc($i)
    end while
  else
    %_legato_data_sus_fade_in_time_offset[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($vlue_authoring_start_note * 25) + (abs($vlue_authoring_end_note - $vlue_authoring_start_note) + (- sh_right(- ($vlue_authoring_end_note - $vlue_authoring_start_note), 31) * 12)))] := $sli_sustain_fadeIn_offset
  end if
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_sustain_fadeIn), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, int((real($sli_sustain_fadeIn) / 1000000.) * 500.) & " + " & int((real($sli_sustain_fadeIn_offset) / 1000000.) * 500.) & " ms")
end on
on ui_control($btn_save_authoring)
  if($authoring_page_active = 1)
    $group_count000 := 0
    $string02 := 0
    $ii4 := 0
    call move_to_legato_buffer
    @legato_name1 := "leg" & %_loaded_subarticulations[0]
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_fade_in_time.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_release_time.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_wait_time.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_in_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_trans_fade_in_time.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_trans_fade_out_time.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_start, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_trans_zone_start.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_volume, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_trans_zone_wait.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_fade_in_time_offset.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_release_time_offset.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_wait_time_offset.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_in_time_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_trans_fade_in_time_offset.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_trans_fade_out_time_offset.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_start_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_trans_zone_start_offset.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_volume_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_trans_zone_wait_offset.nka")
  else
    message("No Legato Loaded")
  end if
  $btn_save_authoring := 0
end on

  if($authoring_page_active = 1)
    !legato_name0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] := "leg" & %_loaded_subarticulations[0]
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & !legato_name0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] & "_sus_fade_in_time.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & !legato_name0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] & "_sus_release_time.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & !legato_name0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] & "_sus_wait_time.nka"))

    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & !legato_name0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] & "_sus_trans_fade_out_time.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_start, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & !legato_name0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] & "_sus_trans_zone_start.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_volume, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & !legato_name0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] & "_sus_trans_zone_volume.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & !legato_name0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] & "_sus_fade_in_time_offset.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & !legato_name0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] & "_sus_release_time_offset.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & !legato_name0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] & "_sus_wait_time.nka_offset"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_in_time_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & !legato_name0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] & "_sus_trans_fade_in_time_offset.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & !legato_name0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] & "_sus_trans_fade_out_time_offset.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_start_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & !legato_name0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] & "_sus_trans_zone_start_offset.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_volume_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & !legato_name0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] & "_sus_trans_zone_volume_offset.nka"))
    $result1500 := 0
    $i1200 := 0
    $result150 := 0
    call move_legato_buffer_to_instrument
    $idx25 := 60
    $subarticulation_event1 := 60
    $iii1 := 0

  end if
  $btn_load_authoring := 0
end on
